Alternative"] || "", fitnessFad: "No", isPremium: index % 4 === 0 // Mocking premium items })); }; const defaultFoodDatabase = processDatabase(defaultRawDatabase); const extractDoshaText = (text, targetDosha) => { if (!text) return ""; const parts = text.split(/(Vata:|Pitta:|Kapha:)/i); for (let i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) { if (parts[i].toLowerCase() === targetDosha.toLowerCase() + ":") { return parts[i+1] ? parts[i+1].trim() : text; } } return text; }; const extractMacrosFromText = (nutText) => { if(!nutText) return { cals: 0, pro: 0, carbs: 0, fats: 0, micros: "" }; const calMatch = nutText.match(/(\d+)\s*Cal/i); const proMatch = nutText.match(/(\d+)g\s*P/i); const carbMatch = nutText.match(/(\d+)g\s*C/i); const fatMatch = nutText.match(/(\d+)g\s*F/i); const microsMatch = nutText.match(/Micros:\s*([^.]*)/i); return { cals: calMatch ? parseInt(calMatch[1]) : 0, pro: proMatch ? parseInt(proMatch[1]) : 0, carbs: carbMatch ? parseInt(carbMatch[1]) : 0, fats: fatMatch ? parseInt(fatMatch[1]) : 0, micros: microsMatch ? microsMatch[1].trim() : "" }; }; const getRecommendedDishes = (dosha, diet, cuisine, country, region, activeDb, cravingDishName) => { const isVegDiet = diet === "Vegetarian" || diet === "Vegan" || diet === "Eggetarian (Veg + Eggs)"; const isVegan = diet === "Vegan"; let safeDishes = activeDb.filter(d => { if (isVegan && d.vegNonVeg !== "Veg" && d.vegNonVeg !== "Veg (Vegan)") return false; if (isVegDiet && d.vegNonVeg.includes("Non-Veg") && !d.vegNonVeg.includes("Egg") && !d.vegNonVeg.includes("Dairy")) return false; const altText = } return true; }); if (safeDishes.length < 3) safeDishes = activeDb; safeDishes.sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random()); safeDishes.sort((a, b) => { let scoreA = 0; let scoreB = 0; if (a.cuisine.includes(cuisine)) scoreA += 2; if (b.cuisine.includes(cuisine)) scoreB += 2; if (a.country === country) scoreA += 1; if (b.country === country) scoreB += 1; return scoreB - scoreA; }); !isBreakfast(d)); if (breakfasts.length === 0) breakfasts = safeDishes; if (mains.length < 2) mains = safeDishes; let selectedCravingDish = null; if (cravingDishName) { selectedCravingDish = activeDb.find(d => d.dishName === cravingDishName); } const bDish = breakfasts[0] || safeDishes[0]; const lDish = selectedCravingDish || mains[0] || safeDishes[1 % safeDishes.length]; const dDish = mains.find(m => m.dishName !== lDish.dishName) || mains[1] || safeDishes[2 % safeDishes.length]; return [bDish, lDish, dDish]; }; const generateRecipeFromDB = (dish, dosha, fullLocationString) => { parsedMacros = extractMacrosFromText(nutritionText); const doshaCap = dosha.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + dosha.slice(1); return { title: `${dish.dishName} (${doshaCap}-Aligned)`, country: dish.country || const generateDynamicMealPlan = (dosha, goal, cuisine, diet, country, region, finalWeightKg, finalHeightCm, activityLevel, activeDb, cravingDishName) => { const heightM = finalHeightCm / 100; const bmi = (finalWeightKg / (heightM * heightM)).toFixed(1); let bmiCategory = "Normal"; if (bmi < 18.5) bmiCategory = "Underweight"; else if (bmi >= 25 && bmi < 29.9) bmiCategory = "Overweight"; else if (bmi >= 30) bmiCategory = "Obese"; const bmr = (10 * finalWeightKg) + (6.25 * finalHeightCm) - 50; const activityMultipliers = { "Sedentary": 1.2, "Lightly Active": 1.375, "Moderately Active": 1.55, "Very Active": 1.725 }; let tdee = bmr * (activityMultipliers[activityLevel] || 1.375); let targetCals = Math.max(1200, Math.round(tdee)); if (goal.includes("Weight Loss")) targetCals -= 500; if (goal.includes("Muscle Gain")) targetCals += 300; const targetProtein = Math.round((targetCals * 0.20) / 4); const targetCarbs = Math.round((targetCals * 0.50) / 4); const targetFats = Math.round((targetCals * 0.30) / 9); const fullLocationString = `${country} ${region}`; const recommendedDishes = getRecommendedDishes(dosha, diet, cuisine, country, region, activeDb, cravingDishName); const bDishRecipe = generateRecipeFromDB(recommendedDishes[0], dosha, fullLocationString); const lDishRecipe = generateRecipeFromDB(recommendedDishes[1], dosha, fullLocationString); const dDishRecipe = generateRecipeFromDB(recommendedDishes[2], dosha, fullLocationString); const menuTotalCals = (bDishRecipe.macros.cals + lDishRecipe.macros.cals + dDishRecipe.macros.cals) || targetCals; const menuTotalPro = (bDishRecipe.macros.pro + lDishRecipe.macros.pro + dDishRecipe.macros.pro) || targetProtein; const timings = { vata: { wake: "6:00 AM", yoga: "6:30 AM", breakfast: dosha, goal: goal, bmiContext: { bmi, category: bmiCategory, weight: Math.round(finalWeightKg), height: Math.round(finalHeightCm), activity: activityLevel, targetCals, targetProtein, targetCarbs, targetFats, menuTotalCals, menuTotalPro }, geoContext: { region: detectRegion(fullLocationString) }, times: timings[dosha] || timings.vata, yogaProtocol: { pranayama: {name: "Anulom Vilom", desc:
